# 219th Battalion B&W

{% raw %}

Canadian Expeditionary<br>
Force<br>
219th BATTALION<br>

Officers and Men.<br>
*<br>
EMBARKATION<br>
Port: Halifax, N.S.<br>
Ship: S.S. "Olympic."<br>
Date: October 12th, 1916.
